<p></p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full is-resized"><img decoding="async" loading="lazy" src="./All known physical attacks on Bitcoin and other cryptocurrencies from 2014 to 2022 - CRYPTO DEEP TECH_files/image-156.png" alt="All known physical attacks on Bitcoin and other cryptocurrencies from 2014 to 2022" class="wp-image-966" width="888" height="1108" srcset="https://cryptodeeptech.ru/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/image-156.png 665w, https://cryptodeeptech.ru/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/image-156-240x300.png 240w" sizes="(max-width: 888px) 100vw, 888px"></figure></div>


<p></p>



<p>A cryptocurrency trader was robbed of more than HK$3 million (US$128,500) in cash at knifepoint when he went to meet a&nbsp;</p>



<p><a href="https://archive.is/o/CeCA8/https://www.scmp.com/topics/bitcoin" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">bitcoin</a></p>



<p>&nbsp;seller in Hong Kong on Wednesday afternoon.</p>



<p>The 39-year-old trader from South Korea arrived at Astoria Building on Ashley Road in Tsim Sha Tsui for the exchange at about 6.20pm. He was approached by four men, one of whom attacked him with the knife.</p>



<p>The criminals snatched a bag he was carrying with about HK$3.29 million inside and fled. The trader asked a friend to call police and officers searched the area but failed to locate the suspects.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter"><img decoding="async" src="./All known physical attacks on Bitcoin and other cryptocurrencies from 2014 to 2022 - CRYPTO DEEP TECH_files/7bcf52cbd67595c34a431487e9683b4dc7207762.webp" alt="Astoria Building on Ashley Road in Tsim Sha Tsui. Photo: Handout"></figure></div>


<p>Astoria Building on Ashley Road in Tsim Sha Tsui. Photo: Handout</p>



<p>The victim suffered a cut to his hand and was sent to hospital for treatment. Detectives from the Yau Tsim district crime squad are investigating.</p>



<p>Several robberies involving digital currency have taken place in Hong Kong this year. In June, a 22-year-old cryptocurrency trader was sprayed in his eyes with an unknown substance and robbed of HK$2 million while on his way to buy the digital money in Kwun Tong. Three men and a woman were later arrested.</p>



<p>In March, two employees of an exchange company were lured to a Tin Hau shop and conned out of HK$3.85 million in a bitcoin transaction scam.</p>



<p>In January, two cryptocurrency traders were robbed of HK$6.5 million in total in two separate cases in the space of a fortnight.</p>



<p>On January 4, a gang tricked a 37-year-old man into transferring more than HK$3 million in bitcoin to them. They paid the victim with cash but took it straight back after he made the transfer. He was left on a hillside on Tai Tam Road in Chai Wan.</p>



<p>Two weeks later, another gang lured a female trader to an office in Kwun Tong for a transaction and robbed her of HK$3.5 million at knifepoint.</p>



<hr class="wp-block-separator has-alpha-channel-opacity">



<figure class="wp-block-table"><table class="has-background" style="background-color:#f78da812"><tbody><tr><td>August ?, 2021</td><td>3 women</td><td>Dubai, United Arab Emirates</td><td><a href="https://archive.is/3dubt" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">4 Africans rob three women of $100,000 in a fake Bitcoin deal</a></td></tr></tbody></table></figure>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full is-resized"><img decoding="async" loading="lazy" src="./All known physical attacks on Bitcoin and other cryptocurrencies from 2014 to 2022 - CRYPTO DEEP TECH_files/image-157.png" alt="All known physical attacks on Bitcoin and other cryptocurrencies from 2014 to 2022" class="wp-image-967" width="867" height="776" srcset="https://cryptodeeptech.ru/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/image-157.png 732w, https://cryptodeeptech.ru/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/image-157-300x269.png 300w" sizes="(max-width: 867px) 100vw, 867px"></figure></div>


<p></p>



<p>Mohammed Yassen,&nbsp;<em>Staff Reporter</em></p>



<p>The Dubai Criminal Court has sentenced a gang of 4 Africans, including a fugitive to one year in prison and ordered them to pay jointly a fine of Dhs342,000 over the charges of robbery under knife-point.</p>



<p>All of them will be deported after serving their jail term.</p>



<p>The details of the cases dates back to when the convicts lured the victims (three women) to a fake deal to sell “Bitcoin.”</p>



<p>Earlier in last August, three women lodged a complaint stating that they had been subjected to robbery under knifepoint by African persons.</p>



<p>One of the victims said in the investigations that an African man offered her to buy cryptocurrency for Dhs300,000, and she accepted the offer and agreed to meet in Al Nahda, Dubai, she added, noting that she accompanied by two of her friends reached the specified location in time.</p>



<p>After waiting for few minutes in a car owned by one of them, the women were surprised by four persons threatening them with blunt objects, ordering them to hand over the money they brought for the cryptocurrency deal.</p>



<p>They gangsters were able to snatch the bag that contained Dhs300,000, in addition to another containing Dhs63,000, other valuable items and their passports as well.</p>



<p>The driver of one of the three women stated in his testimony that he was waiting inside one of the women’s vehicles after they reached the scene, where he heard screaming and saw two Africans threatening the three women, stealing bags and items and fleeing the place in another vehicle.</p>



<p>The driver was able to write down the plate number of the vehicle in which they ran away.</p>



<p>An investigation team managed to identify one of the suspects, as his photo was shown to the victims, who recognised him.</p>



<p>He was arrested and admitted to his presence at the crime scene at the request of one of his friends who asked to drop him to Al Nahda area to complete a “Bitcoin deal.”</p>



<p>They went to the same location at the specified time, as they committed the crime and were able to steal the value of the fake deal, he added.</p>



<p>He also informed the the police about the location of his partners, so two others were arrested, and referred to the Court, where they have been sentenced to one year in jail with a fine equal to the stolen money, in addition to deportation after serving the term.</p>



<hr class="wp-block-separator has-alpha-channel-opacity">



<figure class="wp-block-table"><table class="has-background" style="background-color:#f78da812"><tbody><tr><td>August 8, 2021</td><td>Wesley Pessano Santarem</td><td>Sao Pedro da Aldeia, Brazil</td><td><a href="https://archive.is/2kfpq" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Crypto Trader’s Murder Blamed On Social Media Bragging</a></td></tr></tbody></table></figure>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full is-resized"><img decoding="async" loading="lazy" src="./All known physical attacks on Bitcoin and other cryptocurrencies from 2014 to 2022 - CRYPTO DEEP TECH_files/image-158.png" alt="All known physical attacks on Bitcoin and other cryptocurrencies from 2014 to 2022" class="wp-image-968" width="885" height="838" srcset="https://cryptodeeptech.ru/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/image-158.png 780w, https://cryptodeeptech.ru/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/image-158-300x284.png 300w, https://cryptodeeptech.ru/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/image-158-768x728.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 885px) 100vw, 885px"></figure></div>


<p>The 19-year-old has gained a significant following on Instagram, where he had&nbsp;<a href="https://www.instagram.com/_pessano/?utm_source=ig_embed" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">amassed</a>&nbsp;about 134,000 followers. He also ran an account on YouTube where he published videos in which he offered investment advice.</p>



<p>Pessano was gunned down in broad daylight. He was rolling in his Porsche Boxster sports car through the streets of Sao Pedro da Aldeia, a city in Brazil’s south-eastern state of Rio de Janeiro, to get a haircut, as&nbsp;<a href="https://www.independent.co.uk/news/world/americas/crime/cryptocurrency-bitcoin-trader-killing-porsche-b1899809.html" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">reported</a>&nbsp;by The Independent, when he was ambushed by a group of killers who travelled in a silver Volkswagen.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter"><img decoding="async" src="./All known physical attacks on Bitcoin and other cryptocurrencies from 2014 to 2022 - CRYPTO DEEP TECH_files/25a220723b.png" alt="All known physical attacks on Bitcoin and other cryptocurrencies from 2014 to 2022"><figcaption class="wp-element-caption">Source: _pessano / Instagram</figcaption></figure></div>


<p>A second passenger who sat in his Porsche was injured in the shooting and later transported to a hospital. The Brazilian police said Passano was hit by a minimum of four bullets, one of which was a headshot. An investigation into the murder has been initiated.</p>



<p>Claiming to have secured financial freedom at the age of 18, Pessano often portrayed himself driving luxury cars, among others a Chevrolet Camaro and a Mercedes-Benz automobile. On one of the pictures, the trader was&nbsp;<a href="https://www.instagram.com/p/CMR_EngBvB8/?utm_source=ig_web_copy_link" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">seen</a>&nbsp;‘talking’ on the so-called money phone, pretending to be making a call from a thick stack of cash. This type of photos, as is argued, may have potentially attracted unwanted attention to Pessano’s finances.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter"><img decoding="async" src="./All known physical attacks on Bitcoin and other cryptocurrencies from 2014 to 2022 - CRYPTO DEEP TECH_files/259f060449.png" alt="All known physical attacks on Bitcoin and other cryptocurrencies from 2014 to 2022"><figcaption class="wp-element-caption">Source: _pessano / Instagram</figcaption></figure></div>


<p>The latest violent event joins a worrying string of gruesome attacks on crypto traders that has been observed worldwide.</p>



<p>Last January, a trader in Hong Kong was&nbsp;<a href="https://cryptonews.com/news/teaching-true-story-trader-robbed-of-nearly-usd-half-million-8809.htm">robbed</a>&nbsp;of nearly half a million dollars worth of&nbsp;<a href="https://cryptonews.com/coins/bitcoin/">bitcoin (BTC)</a>. A Norwegian trader was&nbsp;<a href="https://cryptonews.com/news/bitcoin-millionaire-jumps-from-window-to-escape-burglar-4609.htm">forced</a>&nbsp;to jump from a window of his house last year when an armed man showed up at his door. The same year in the Netherlands, crypto community was&nbsp;<a href="https://cryptonews.com/news/crypto-community-talk-guns-after-another-brutal-robbery-3428.htm">shocked</a>&nbsp;by a brutal robbery attempt in which three armed robbers with police vests broke into a residential building and tortured a 38-year-old trader for over an hour using a drill. In 2018, a Norwegian trader was&nbsp;<a href="https://cryptonews.com/news/norwegian-man-stabbed-to-death-after-in-person-bitcoin-sale-2790.htm">found</a>&nbsp;dead in his apartment in Oslo after selling bitcoins to another person for cash.</p>



<p>And these are just a few of many reported attacks, threatening crypto traders’/holders’ personal safety. It is not clear how many crypto-related attacks or attempted attacks have gone unreported.</p>



<p></p>



<hr class="wp-block-separator has-alpha-channel-opacity">



<figure class="wp-block-table"><table class="has-background" style="background-color:#f78da812"><tbody><tr><td>August 18, 2021</td><td>Simon Arthuis</td><td>Plancher-Bas, France</td><td><a href="https://archive.md/7mvSY" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Computer engineering student killed for €200,000 in cryptocurrency</a></td></tr></tbody></table></figure>



<h1>Assassination in Plancher-Bas: the student killed for 200,000 € of cryptocurrency</h1>



<p>The body of a 19-year-old young man with twenty stab wounds was discovered last August in a pond in Plancher-Bas, in Haute-Saône.&nbsp;Two months after the preventive incarceration of the first three suspects, a couple was arrested, indicted and imprisoned for complicity in murder.&nbsp;All dreamed of stealing €200,000 of cryptocurrency belonging to Simon Arthuis, their victim, reveals the Besançon prosecutor.By&nbsp;</p>



<p><strong>Willy GRAFF</strong>&nbsp;–&nbsp;</p>



<p>Oct 22, 2021, 7:12 PM |&nbsp;updated yesterday at 09:24 – Reading time:&nbsp;3 min</p>



<p><sub></sub>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;|&nbsp;&nbsp;Seen 37482 times</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter"><a href="https://archive.md/o/7mvSY/https://cdn-s-www.estrepublicain.fr/images/BE50552F-D86B-4DEE-A749-9CAA3193D5CF/NW_raw/le-corps-d-un-jeune-homme-de-19-ans-avait-ete-decouvert-le-18-aout-2021-dans-un-etang-de-plancher-bas-en-haute-saone-photo-d-archives-er-1634922770.jpg" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener"><img decoding="async" src="./All known physical attacks on Bitcoin and other cryptocurrencies from 2014 to 2022 - CRYPTO DEEP TECH_files/56cc28d8476efe9d9fb4af8cf22f830e4b46775d.jpg" alt="All known physical attacks on Bitcoin and other cryptocurrencies from 2014 to 2022"></a></figure></div>


<p>It is a staggering affair, both in its extreme cruelty and in its basely villainous nature.&nbsp;The public prosecutor of Besançon detailed this Friday the underside of the investigation opened following&nbsp;</p>



<p><a href="https://archive.md/o/7mvSY/https://www.estrepublicain.fr/faits-divers-justice/2021/08/19/un-jeune-homme-retrouve-tue-par-arme-blanche-pres-d-un-etang" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">the discovery of a tortured body</a>&nbsp;, larded with about twenty stab wounds, on August 18 in a pond in Plancher-Bas ( Haute-Saone).&nbsp;That of Simon Arthuis, a 19-year-old uneventful computer engineering student, residing in Tours.</p>



<h2>Three quick arrests</h2>



<p>The first three men, the victim’s lover, a 33-year-old from Montbéliard, and two individuals aged 18 and 23,&nbsp;</p>



<p><a href="https://archive.md/o/7mvSY/https://www.estrepublicain.fr/faits-divers-justice/2021/08/19/meurtre-a-plancher-bas-un-homme-de-19-ans-tue-d-une-vingtaine-de-coups-de-couteau" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">were quickly placed in police custody</a>&nbsp;, then indicted&nbsp;</p>



<p><a href="https://archive.md/o/7mvSY/https://www.estrepublicain.fr/faits-divers-justice/2021/08/20/meurtre-de-plancher-bas-trois-hommes-suspectes-d-assassinat" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">for murder</a>&nbsp;.&nbsp;A notion that implies the premeditation of the crime.&nbsp;“They all three admit to being involved in the death of this 19-year-old young man, even if no one admits having given the fatal blows”, recalls the prosecutor Étienne Manteaux.&nbsp;The companion of the deceased had initially tried to cover his tracks, by telling the gendarmes the scenario of an attack of a homophobic nature, from which he alone would have survived.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter"><a href="https://archive.md/o/7mvSY/https://cdn-s-www.estrepublicain.fr/images/0a7e7461-928e-482b-913d-4055a6ae86b3/NW_raw/pour-le-procureur-etienne-manteaux-le-couple-interpelle-ce-mercredi-minimise-son-role-dans-la-planification-de-l-homicide-photo-er-franck-hakmoun-1634922770.jpg" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener"><img decoding="async" src="./All known physical attacks on Bitcoin and other cryptocurrencies from 2014 to 2022 - CRYPTO DEEP TECH_files/04d203018711c12bae8ff50d088a11af2736d3d3.jpg" alt="All known physical attacks on Bitcoin and other cryptocurrencies from 2014 to 2022"></a><figcaption class="wp-element-caption">For prosecutor Étienne Manteaux, the couple arrested on Wednesday “minimises” their role in the planning of the homicide.&nbsp;Photo ER /FRANCK HAKMOUN</figcaption></figure></div>


<h2>A couple presumed to be accomplices, but to what extent?</h2>



<p>The complex case has just taken a new turn.&nbsp;The bloodhounds of the research section (SR) of Besançon arrested this Wednesday, October 20 two new people: the twin brother of the lover and his companion.&nbsp;What is the real role played by this couple?&nbsp;Future investigations must still lift the veil.“After denying it, they too acknowledged their involvement, while minimizing it.&nbsp;They admit to having been informed of the project before the death of the victim and not to have denounced it”, indicates the prosecutor.&nbsp;Both were indicted for complicity in murder and remanded in custody.</p>



<h2>200,000 euros of cryptocurrency in the viewfinder</h2>



<p><a href="https://archive.md/o/7mvSY/https://www.estrepublicain.fr/faits-divers-justice/2021/08/21/meurtre-de-plancher-bas-les-trois-suspects-ecroues" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">The motive for this terrible ambush</a>&nbsp;is assumed: to extort money from this young engineer.&nbsp;“He had created software for stock trading”, specifies the colonel of gendarmerie Yves Raguin, generating on his account “about 200,000 € of different cryptocurrencies, including Bitcoin”.The five suspects, from a very modest social condition, admit having tricked him to steal him.&nbsp;“But as soon as we go into detail, their versions diverge,” notes the prosecutor.</p>



<h2>Thrown dying in the pond</h2>



<p>According to Étienne Manteaux, the autopsy reveals some macabre clues: “The very many blows observed between the sternum and the lower part of the face can attest to a session of torture or a gesture of passion.&nbsp;We also know that none of these blows were fatal in themselves, and that the victim was dying when he was thrown into the pond”.Another incriminating element for the recently imprisoned couple: the victim had of his own free will lunch on August 18 at noon at their home in Plancher-les-Mines.&nbsp;Where she would have been drugged, according to the first three suspects.&nbsp;“Toxicological analyzes are in progress to confirm it”, prolongs the prosecutor.&nbsp;The woman in question will also have to explain herself about the opening of a Boursorama account in her name… A few days before the assassination of the young cryptocurrency holder.</p>



<hr class="wp-block-separator has-alpha-channel-opacity">



<figure class="wp-block-table"><table class="has-background" style="background-color:#f78da812"><tbody><tr><td>September ?, 2021</td><td>Unidentified 31 y/o</td><td>Abkhazia</td><td><a href="https://archive.is/MPNwC" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Thieves break into garage, steal 20 mining servers worth $10,000.</a></td></tr></tbody></table></figure>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="1024" height="684" src="./All known physical attacks on Bitcoin and other cryptocurrencies from 2014 to 2022 - CRYPTO DEEP TECH_files/image-159-1024x684.png" alt="All known physical attacks on Bitcoin and other cryptocurrencies from 2014 to 2022" class="wp-image-971" srcset="https://cryptodeeptech.ru/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/image-159-1024x684.png 1024w, https://cryptodeeptech.ru/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/image-159-300x200.png 300w, https://cryptodeeptech.ru/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/image-159-768x513.png 768w, https://cryptodeeptech.ru/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/image-159.png 1073w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px"></figure></div>


<p class="has-text-align-center has-large-font-size"><strong>Abkhazia’s illegal bitcoin miners face new threat from thieves</strong></p>



<p>TBILISI, Jan 6 (Thomson Reuters Foundation) – When Valeri checked the Abkhazia garage where he had set up a small and illegal bitcoin mining operation one autumn morning, he found the door bust open. Thieves had broken in overnight, taking with them 20 mining servers worth about $10,000.</p>



<p>“They cleaned up the place completely,” said the 31-year-old from the Black Sea region, who preferred not to use his real name, adding the robbery left him feeling “angry and frustrated”.</p>



<p>His was no isolated case. Cryptocurrency miners say Abkhazia has been hit by a wave of burglaries – some of them violent – since authorities banned the power-intensive activity to stem an energy crisis in 2020.</p>



<p>In October, five men armed with guns and Kalashnikov rifles accidentally killed one of their own after opening fire on thieves who had broken into a country house to steal mining servers, according to the local prosecutor’s office.</p>



<p>And last month police said they made one arrest after two masked men broke into a home in Sukhumi, the capital, and held a family at gunpoint before escaping with three servers and 150,000 roubles ($2,040) in cash.</p>



<p>The wave of thefts is the latest twist in the region’s crypto world, which many locals see as one of few ways to make ends meet.</p>



<p>Abkhazia broke away from Georgia in the early 1990s after the collapse of the Soviet Union.</p>



<p>It is recognised as an independent state only by Russia, which has a military presence there, and a handful of other nations, leaving it largely isolated and underdeveloped.</p>



<p>“If conditions in our small republic were better than they are now, then I would do something else,” said Victor, a 34-year-old bitcoin miner who asked to protect his identity.</p>



<p>POWER TROUBLES</p>



<p>A lush strip of land once the playground of the Soviet elite, Abkhazia experienced a mining boom last year as bitcoin prices soared.</p>



<p>Bitcoins are generated in a process called “mining”, in which a global network of computers competes to solve complex algorithms.</p>



<p>These computers require a vast amount of energy to run, with climate experts voicing concerns about cryptocurrencies’ potential to derail efforts to tackle global warming.</p>



<p>The crypto craze put Abkhazia’s outdated energy system on the ropes, triggering outages and causing overloaded power stations to catch fire – which led to the government’s latest mining ban in December 2020.</p>



<p>Police went on the hunt for crypto farms, raiding homes, attics, and even restaurants – cutting the power cables to mining processors they found. In March the government imposed new hefty fines on offenders.</p>



<p>Abkhazia’s interior ministry told the Thomson Reuters Foundation it has opened “specialised” and “secured” warehouses to hold mining devices seized by authorities, as well as a hotline to report suspicious activity.</p>



<p>The government credited the crackdown with easing pressure on the energy grid through the summer – but the crisis did not abate, with energy consumption rising again in the autumn.</p>



<p>In October, Abkhazia’s energy company Chernomorenergo pleaded with all residents to “reduce consumption as much as possible”, as it announced new rolling blackouts.</p>



<p>“The ban has not worked at all. It’s as simple as that,” said Michael Lambert, a political psychologist and non-resident associate at the OSCE Academy in Bishkek, Kyrgyzstan, who has written about the issue.</p>



<p>Neither Abkhazia’s economy ministry nor the prosecutor’s office replied to requests for comment.</p>



<p>Energy in Abkhazia is so cheap that despite the government crackdown mining has proven too tempting for many locals, said Lambert.</p>



<p>Suspicion that government officials are in on the business has done little to persuade miners to pull the plug, added Maximilian Hess, a research fellow at the Foreign Policy Research Institute, a U.S. think tank.</p>



<p>“The region has long been attractive to organised crime and for corruption,” he said. “Any crackdown locally will not necessarily be perceived as an act of law, but as various factions … playing against one another.”</p>



<p>In February the aide to a lawmaker was fired after being caught smuggling mining equipment from Russia aboard a government-owned car, in a case that sparked local outrage.</p>



<p>“I will stop doing this only when representatives of our government liquidate their own crypto farms,” said Victor.</p>



<p>DIY SECURITY</p>



<p>Unable to turn to the police for help due to the illegal nature of their business, crypto miners have resorted to their own means of protection.</p>



<p>After a botched burglary, Victor said he fitted the disbanded factory warehouse where he holds some 140 servers worth about $72,000 with indoor and outdoor cameras, motion sensors and a remote notification system.</p>



<p>“It cost me about $2,000,” he said, adding violent incidents like the shooting in October were an “exception”.</p>



<p>“Server thefts are widespread … but mostly carried out by young people because of low living standards and lack of employment”.</p>



<p>The robbers who tried to break into his warehouse earlier this year fled as soon as the alarm went off, he said.</p>



<p>Valeri, who had no such security measures in place, said he has tried to track down the thieves himself but to no avail.</p>



<p>“I have another job but mining was my main income,” he said. “This is a very good business that I really want to do again. Unfortunately now I have no money to buy the equipment.”</p>



<p>LOOKING FOR SOLUTIONS</p>



<p>The crypto mining crisis has become increasingly difficult for authorities to handle, with continuing power cuts causing widespread anger.</p>



<p>“The population is rightly indignant, and their indignation is quite understandable,” Abkhazia President Aslan Bzhania told a government meeting in November.</p>



<p>Days later, a gunman fired several shots at the headquarters of energy company Chernomorenergo, before being arrested, the interior ministry said on its website.</p>



<p>While police did not disclose a motive, the shooter was hailed a hero by disgruntled locals on social media, according to local news.</p>



<p>Abkhazia gets most of its power from a massive Soviet-era dam it shares with Georgia which underwent repairs earlier this year and, like most hydroelectric plants, sees low water levels in winter when demand for energy is higher.</p>



<p>To make up for the shortfall, the government has been importing energy from Russia, increasing its dependence on the Kremlin – causing concern among the more independent-minded Abkhaz, said Lambert.</p>



<p>Last month, opposition parties organised a large protest in Sukhumi against the government’s handling of the energy crisis, among other issues.</p>



<p>The government has laid out plans to renovate the energy grid, set up a new system to calculate and levy electricity tariffs and create a “technopark” where miners could operate legally.</p>



<p>But Victor is sceptical.</p>



<p>“For almost 30 years after the war, our government could not or did not want to restore water supply and energy infrastructure. So I do not really understand what technopark we are talking about.”</p>



<hr class="wp-block-separator has-alpha-channel-opacity">



<figure class="wp-block-table"><table class="has-background" style="background-color:#f78da812"><tbody><tr><td>September 9, 2021</td><td>Mark Geor</td><td>Westmere, New Zealand</td><td><a href="https://archive.md/y8m24" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Safe containing $4M of cryptocurrency ripped from house</a></td></tr></tbody></table></figure>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full is-resized"><img decoding="async" loading="lazy" src="./All known physical attacks on Bitcoin and other cryptocurrencies from 2014 to 2022 - CRYPTO DEEP TECH_files/image-160.png" alt="All known physical attacks on Bitcoin and other cryptocurrencies from 2014 to 2022" class="wp-image-972" width="912" height="882" srcset="https://cryptodeeptech.ru/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/image-160.png 819w, https://cryptodeeptech.ru/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/image-160-300x290.png 300w, https://cryptodeeptech.ru/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/image-160-768x743.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 912px) 100vw, 912px"></figure></div>


<p>A wealthy businessman is offering a hefty reward of $500,000 in return for a stolen safe containing $4 million in cryptocurrency.</p>



<p>Mark Geor previously told the Weekend Herald his family home in the Auckland suburb of Westmere was burgled while it was being renovated.</p>



<p>He said the thieves took an extraordinary haul including $10,000 in cash, Rolex and Tag Hauer watches, diamond jewellery and family heirlooms.</p>



<p>Private investigator Mike Campbell believes the burglary happened between 8.30pm and midnight on 9-10 September.</p>



<p>Campbell told the Weekend Herald; the substantial reward was an appeal to the culprits to return all the contents from the safe.</p>



<p>“We’ve been down a couple of paths but they’ve fizzled out. One of the dangers of this you get people ringing up who are economical with the truth which is all part of the process. We believe the cryptocurrency hasn’t been touched yet and nobody has come forward about the safe being blown up. The feeling is, talking to the odd criminal, the safe is sitting around somewhere. Someone out there knows something,” Campbell said.</p>



<p>Reward poster for Mark and Clare Geor. Their house was burgled in Westmere and $4 million dollars of crypto currency was stolen in a safe. Photo / Supplied</p>



<p>He said CCTV footage from a neighbour’s security cameras revealed possible suspects driving a white Subaru Legacy wagon and a 2005 Toyota Ute with a hood on the back between 9pm and 9.30pm.</p>



<p>One neighbour noticed a potential suspect in the neighbourhood two days before the burglary.</p>



<p>“The safe was bolted to the concrete floor and weighs about 160 kilos so you’d need a big strong person to cut it away and shift it out of the cupboard in the stairwell,” Campbell said.</p>



<p>“They had to drag it across the room and put it in a wheelbarrow to take it to the front of the house and have a vehicle big enough to carry the safe.”</p>



<p>It is the first cryptocurrency theft Campbell has been involved in the 40 years he’s been a private investigator.</p>



<h4>ADVERTISEMENT</h4>



<p><a href="https://archive.md/o/y8m24/https://advertising.nzme.co.nz/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Advertise with NZME.</a></p>



<p>On September 10 when Geor went to collect the mail, he noticed a builder’s wheelbarrow with a pillow on it.</p>



<p>He discovered the house had been broken into and burglars had entered through a side door, where there were no security cameras.</p>



<p>“They turned off the power and disarmed my alarm and backup battery. The electrical switchboard, control box for the alarm was in the same room as the safe. If you set the alarm there is a wee delay before it goes off, it looks like they were able to shut it off pretty quickly, so they knew what they were doing,” Geor said.</p>



<p>Campbell told the Weekend Herald rewards can be helpful in solving crimes.</p>



<p>“Burglars often get rid of stuff pretty quickly or they hang on to it until things cool down. Rewards are generally associated with the value of the information. In this case, it’s the data that relates to the cryptocurrency,” Campbell said.</p>



<p>He is urging the public to call 0800 384 4227 with information.</p>



<p>A police spokesperson said, “The matter is still being actively investigated so we can’t comment further at this stage.”</p>



<p>Although there is no evidence the safe has been cracked open or funds have been withdrawn, Geor can’t claim insurance for the cryptocurrency he has lost.</p>



<p>“Unfortunately, there is no such thing as insurance.”</p>



<p>Geor’s message to the raiders in September was simply “GIVE IT BACK.”</p>



<p>“I am gutted, despite the money, I feel stupid for having all my possessions in there. There is nothing fair or reasonable about this, I just want my stuff.”</p>



<p></p>



<hr class="wp-block-separator has-alpha-channel-opacity">



<figure class="wp-block-table"><table class="has-background" style="background-color:#f78da812"><tbody><tr><td>October 7, 2021</td><td>Liquor Store</td><td>South Bay, California</td><td><a href="https://archive.is/1caUw" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Thieves Break Into Liquor Store to Steal Bitcoin ATM</a></td></tr></tbody></table></figure>



<p><a href="https://www.nbcbayarea.com/tag/bitcoin/">BITCOIN</a></p>



<h1>Thieves Break Into Silicon Valley Liquor Store to Steal Bitcoin ATM</h1>



<h4>By&nbsp;<a href="https://www.nbcbayarea.com/?s=Author%3A%20%22Scott%20Budman%22">Scott Budman</a>&nbsp;and&nbsp;<a href="https://www.nbcbayarea.com/?s=Author%3A%20%22Kristofer%20Noceda%22">Kristofer Noceda</a>&nbsp;<strong>•</strong>&nbsp;Published October 8, 2021&nbsp;<strong>•</strong>&nbsp;Updated on&nbsp;October 16, 2021&nbsp;at&nbsp;10:53 pm</h4>



<p><a href="https://www.facebook.com/sharer/sharer.php?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.nbcbayarea.com%2Fnews%2Flocal%2Fthieves-break-into-silicon-valley-liquor-store-to-steal-bitcoin-atm%2F2677196%2F&amp;Thieves%20Break%20Into%20Silicon%20Valley%20Liquor%20Store%20to%20Steal%20Bitcoin%20ATM?_osource=db_npd_nbc_kntv_fb_shr" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener"></a>&nbsp;<a href="https://twitter.com/intent/tweet?text=Thieves%20Break%20Into%20Silicon%20Valley%20Liquor%20Store%20to%20Steal%20Bitcoin%20ATM&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.nbcbayarea.com%2Fnews%2Flocal%2Fthieves-break-into-silicon-valley-liquor-store-to-steal-bitcoin-atm%2F2677196%2F?_osource=db_npd_nbc_kntv_twt_shr" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener"></a>&nbsp;</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full is-resized"><img decoding="async" loading="lazy" src="./All known physical attacks on Bitcoin and other cryptocurrencies from 2014 to 2022 - CRYPTO DEEP TECH_files/image-161.png" alt="All known physical attacks on Bitcoin and other cryptocurrencies from 2014 to 2022" class="wp-image-975" width="896" height="948" srcset="https://cryptodeeptech.ru/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/image-161.png 622w, https://cryptodeeptech.ru/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/image-161-283x300.png 283w" sizes="(max-width: 896px) 100vw, 896px"></figure></div>


<p><a href="mailto:?body=Thieves%20Break%20Into%20Silicon%20Valley%20Liquor%20Store%20to%20Steal%20Bitcoin%20ATM%0D%0A%0D%0Ahttps%3A%2F%2Fwww.nbcbayarea.com%2Fnews%2Flocal%2Fthieves-break-into-silicon-valley-liquor-store-to-steal-bitcoin-atm%2F2677196%2F?_osource=db_npd_nbc_kntv_eml_shr" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener"></a></p>



<h3>Scroll down to watch video.&nbsp;</h3>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter is-resized"><img decoding="async" loading="lazy" src="./All known physical attacks on Bitcoin and other cryptocurrencies from 2014 to 2022 - CRYPTO DEEP TECH_files/CHP-Generics.png" alt="Truck Fire on Dumbarton Bridge Blocks All ..." width="501" height="281"></figure></div>


<p>Surveillance video from a Silicon Valley liquor store shows thieves taking off with a Bitcoin ATM.</p>



<p>The store owner tells NBC Bay Area the incident occurred at 4:50 a.m. Thursday.</p>



<p>Video obtained by NBC Bay Area appears to show the Bitcoin ATM wrapped with a cord and tied to the back of a white van outside the liquor store. The van then drives forward to pull the machine through the front of the store, knocking out a front door.</p>



<blockquote class="wp-block-quote">
<p><a href="https://twitter.com/hashtag/New?src=hash&amp;ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw">#New</a>: Thieves break into Silicon Valley liquor store .. not to steal the cash ATM, but to steal the&nbsp;<a href="https://twitter.com/hashtag/Bitcoin?src=hash&amp;ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw">#Bitcoin</a>&nbsp;ATM.&nbsp;<a href="https://t.co/eISIHokjED">pic.twitter.com/eISIHokjED</a>— scott budman (@scottbudman)&nbsp;<a href="https://twitter.com/scottbudman/status/1446540818316070917?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw">October 8, 2021</a></p>
</blockquote>



<p>Police said they are reviewing the surveillance video and are investigating.</p>



<p>No other information was available on the incident.</p>



<p>Bitcoin ATMs have popped up across the United States over the past year. The machine allows customers to buy or sell the digital currency, and sometimes extract cash, according to a&nbsp;<a rel="noreferrer noopener" href="https://www.reuters.com/article/us-usa-crypto-currencies-atms-idINKBN2B714L" target="_blank">Reuters</a>&nbsp;report on the growing popularity of Bitcoin ATMs.</p>



<p>2:60</p>



<p>Brazen Burglary: Silicon Valley Bitcoin ATM Theft</p>



<p>NBC Bay Area’s Raj Mathai spoke with Business and Tech Reporter Scott Budman about the brazen burglary at a Sunnyvale liquor store.</p>



<p>“Honestly, if I was going after Bitcoin and trying to steal it, I would hack instead,” said Caroline Chen, a business professor at San Jose State University. “Because then I know I can steal millions of dollars of Bitcoin in one fell swoop, instead of the ATM at the local convenience store that has $200 of actual cash in it.”</p>



<p>There are now over 48,000 Bitcoin ATMs across the nation, according to independent research site&nbsp;<a rel="noreferrer noopener" href="https://howmanybitcoinatms.com/" target="_blank">howmanybitcoinatms.com</a>.</p>



<p>Meanwhile, Bitcoin this week bounced back by topping $55,000,&nbsp;<a rel="noreferrer noopener" href="https://www.cnbc.com/2021/10/06/bitcoin-price-above-55k-trader-on-which-cryptocurrency-could-rally.html" target="_blank">CNBC reported</a>. It marked the highest level for the cryptocurrency since mid-May.</p>



<p></p>



<hr class="wp-block-separator has-alpha-channel-opacity">



<figure class="wp-block-table"><table class="has-background" style="background-color:#f78da812"><tbody><tr><td>October 20, 2021</td><td>Astamur Ardzibna</td><td>Abkhazia</td><td><a href="https://archive.is/zg4Kk" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Man Shot Dead in Hail of Gunfire Over Crypto Mining Rigs</a></td></tr></tbody></table></figure>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full is-resized"><img decoding="async" loading="lazy" src="./All known physical attacks on Bitcoin and other cryptocurrencies from 2014 to 2022 - CRYPTO DEEP TECH_files/image-162.png" alt="All known physical attacks on Bitcoin and other cryptocurrencies from 2014 to 2022" class="wp-image-978" width="892" height="828" srcset="https://cryptodeeptech.ru/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/image-162.png 827w, https://cryptodeeptech.ru/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/image-162-300x279.png 300w, https://cryptodeeptech.ru/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/image-162-768x713.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 892px) 100vw, 892px"></figure></div>


<p>On October 20, a man opened fire on people attempting to steal his cryptocurrency mining equipment in the Abkhazia region bordering Russia.&nbsp;<a href="https://archive.is/o/zg4Kk/https://eadaily.com/ru/news/2021/10/25/zhitel-abhazii-pogib-v-boyu-za-oborudovanie-po-dobyche-kriptovalyut" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">According to</a>&nbsp;police, the man killed one of his own friends while fending off the attackers and is now in custody.</p>



<p>Abkhazia is a&nbsp;<a href="https://archive.is/o/zg4Kk/https://www.vice.com/en/article/wjy75w/abkhazia-is-yet-another-country-that-doesnt-exist" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">disputed territory</a>&nbsp;along the Black Sea where officials have been&nbsp;<a href="https://archive.is/o/zg4Kk/https://www.vice.com/en/article/5dpxzn/abkhazia-posts-videos-of-illegal-bitcoin-mines-that-are-causing-power-blackouts" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">fighting cryptocurrency miners</a>&nbsp;for years. Electricity in the country is&nbsp;<a href="https://archive.is/o/zg4Kk/https://www.reuters.com/article/us-georgia-tech-currency-analysis-trfn-idUSKBN2AT1UC" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">ten times cheaper</a>&nbsp;than in neighboring Georgia and miners have flooded the area and stressed the power grid, leading to rolling blackouts. The problem is so bad that Abkhazia&nbsp;<a href="https://archive.is/o/zg4Kk/https://www.reuters.com/article/us-georgia-tech-currency-analysis-trfn-idUSKBN2AT1UC" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">has estimated</a>&nbsp;there is one crypto-mining facility for every 400 residents. Abkhazia&nbsp;<a href="https://archive.is/o/zg4Kk/https://www.vice.com/en/article/5dpxzn/abkhazia-posts-videos-of-illegal-bitcoin-mines-that-are-causing-power-blackouts" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">briefly legalized mining</a>, but then&nbsp;<a href="https://archive.is/o/zg4Kk/https://www.coindesk.com/markets/2021/04/05/abkhazia-bans-bitcoin-mining-shortly-after-legalizing-it/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">outlawed it again this year</a>&nbsp;and began to seize and destroy the machines.</p>



<p>Authorities in Abkhazia have just started the investigation of the cryptocurrency shooting but early reports indicated it was a robbery gone wrong. According to a statement from the General Prosecutor’s Office of Abkhazia, a group of men running a cryptocurrency mining operation in the village of Aatsy tried to stop the theft of their machines by at least five men using Kalashnikov rifles and Makarov pistols. Amid the gunfire, police say that one of the men killed his friend.&nbsp;</p>



<p>“When stopping the theft of equipment for the extraction of cryptocurrency by at least five persons, they opened fire from the available firearms, as a result of which Pachial R.G., realizing the social danger of his actions when firing shots from close range, comitted the murder of A.B. Ardzibna,” the&nbsp;<a href="https://archive.is/o/zg4Kk/https://www.genproc-abh.ru/genproc-news/item/799-prokuraturoj-gudautskogo-rajona-vozbuzhdeno-ugolovnoe-delo-po-faktu-ubjstva-ardzinba-a-b" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">statement said</a>, according to Google translate.</p>



<p>According to&nbsp;<a href="https://archive.is/o/zg4Kk/https://www.ekhokavkaza.com/a/31530659.html" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Echo of the Caucasus</a>, there are conflicting reports about what actually happened during the shooting. The official statement is worded strangely and friends and family of the deceased are keeping quiet so as not to disrupt the investigation, though the outlet notes that it appears indisputable that the shooting occurred around and because of a Bitcoin mine.</p>



<p>“Astamur Ardzinba was killed. A friend, a classmate of my eldest son. A well-mannered young man whom I loved in a fatherly way. I have been broken since yesterday,” Abkhazia&nbsp;<a href="https://archive.is/o/zg4Kk/https://abkhazworld.com/aw/analysis/1880-better-a-bitter-truth-than-a-sweet-lie-by-david-dasania" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">blogger</a>&nbsp;David Dasnia said on his&nbsp;<a href="https://archive.is/o/zg4Kk/https://www.facebook.com/dasania/posts/4590821350982352?__cft__[0]=AZVx2qGWRAXsvnQrdfMNRHjSjX_tfOWZorQXJ1yt3KXSbwFKgZ-YdfDU9OoBRWv_Yef7Vp0Tx9QulmXxfreO3bDuVJVAgfc_NDLksdLd-21H9rFhUEGWTvNWwEeyMPmtw3M&amp;__tn__=,O,P-R" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Facebook page</a>, Echo of the Caucasus reported. “I cry like a child from impotence. Only one thought comes to my mind: what about his father? May his murderers be cursed forever and ever! When will total order be restored in Abkhazia?”</p>



<hr class="wp-block-separator has-alpha-channel-opacity">



<figure class="wp-block-table"><table class="has-background" style="background-color:#f78da812"><tbody><tr><td>November 2, 2021</td><td>Zaryn Dentzel</td><td>Madrid, Spain</td><td><a href="https://archive.md/f5nIJ" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Home invaders torture social media founder, take tens of millions of euros in bitcoin</a></td></tr></tbody></table></figure>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full is-resized"><img decoding="async" loading="lazy" src="./All known physical attacks on Bitcoin and other cryptocurrencies from 2014 to 2022 - CRYPTO DEEP TECH_files/image-163.png" alt="All known physical attacks on Bitcoin and other cryptocurrencies from 2014 to 2022" class="wp-image-981" width="865" height="873" srcset="https://cryptodeeptech.ru/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/image-163.png 788w, https://cryptodeeptech.ru/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/image-163-297x300.png 297w, https://cryptodeeptech.ru/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/image-163-150x150.png 150w, https://cryptodeeptech.ru/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/image-163-768x776.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 865px) 100vw, 865px"></figure></div>


<p>The agents of the Judicial Police of the Superior Headquarters of&nbsp;<a href="https://archive.md/o/f5nIJ/https://www.elespanol.com/organismos/policia_nacional/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">the National Police in Madrid</a>&nbsp;have been investigating since early this afternoon&nbsp;<strong>the robbery and attempted kidnapping</strong>&nbsp;perpetrated against&nbsp;<strong>Zaryn Dentzel,</strong>&nbsp;first president of&nbsp;<a href="https://archive.md/o/f5nIJ/https://www.elespanol.com/organismos/tuenti/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">the Tuenti social network</a>&nbsp;.&nbsp;The creator of this platform has denounced this Tuesday that he had been the&nbsp;<strong>victim of an organized gang</strong>&nbsp;that would have entered his apartment and that, after handcuffing and gagging him, has stolen his laptops, his mobile phone and his tablet.</p>



<p>The victim has told the investigators that after extorting money from him for several hours, the assailants also managed to extract the password of an account in which, he claims, he had&nbsp;</p>



<p><strong>several tens of millions of euros in bitcoin</strong>&nbsp;stored .The events, as EL ESPAÑOL has been able to learn exclusively through judicial and police sources, have taken place in Ruiz de Alarcón, a central street in the capital.&nbsp;Dentzel, who had lived in Spain for a long time, was the owner of the house where the kidnapping would have taken place.This occurred around three in the afternoon.&nbsp;Around that time, according to what Dentzel told the agents, the businessman was in the apartment with a friend and a maintenance worker.&nbsp;A short time later, according to the same sources that the founder of Tuenti reported, the bell was heard.&nbsp;Opening it,&nbsp;</p>



<p><strong>a group of four or five people</strong>&nbsp;appeared .&nbsp;They were all hooded.It was then that they burst into the house.&nbsp;After covering the security cameras that Dentzel had in the house, they handcuffed him, gagged him and sprayed him, always based on the complainant’s account, with a spray in the eyes.&nbsp;</p>



<h3>Extortion and threats</h3>



<p>During the following four hours, the perpetrators of the kidnapping repeatedly beat the owner of the house, making all kinds of threats until they obtained what they needed from him.&nbsp;They made several cuts on his chest and applied electric shocks with a taser gun.&nbsp;Hours later, upon arriving at the apartment, the agents confirmed that he indeed&nbsp;</p>



<p><strong>had wounds perpetrated with a knife</strong>&nbsp;.&nbsp;&nbsp;Thus, until, according to the sources consulted and the victim’s account, he&nbsp;</p>



<p><strong>confessed the password of his bitcoin account in</strong>&nbsp;which he has assured to save a fortune.&nbsp;Apparently, as he confessed to the agents of the Judicial Police Brigade who attended the scene, he had several million euros in that virtual currency in it.&nbsp;After getting what they were looking for, the members of the band would have taken the laptops, the phones, Dentzel’s tablet and also a pen drive.&nbsp;The owner of the house stated that the authors would later go down to the street, without being able to determine the value of what was stolen.&nbsp;The first to alert the National Police was a neighbor who heard cries for help coming from inside the building.&nbsp;Other inhabitants of the same block observed, as they reported to the agents, a group of masked people going down the street, carrying various bags.The first hypotheses that the researchers are considering suggest that, according to the accent of the kidnappers, appreciated by the victims, it could be a gang made up of&nbsp;</p>



<p><strong>criminals from Eastern Europe</strong>&nbsp;.At the moment the Scientific Police is in the house analyzing the crime scene and collecting all kinds of evidence where the events have occurred.&nbsp;The Judicial Police Brigade has also appeared in the apartment and is taking a statement from the founder of the social network.Zaryn was born in 1983 in Santa Barbara, California.&nbsp;In 1998, Zaryn landed in Spain for a study exchange.&nbsp;In 2006 he created Tuenti and became famous and a millionaire in Spain thanks to this successful and popular social network.&nbsp;After selling the platform to Telefónica and after Tuenti closed in 2016, Dentzel has continued to be linked to Spain.&nbsp;Here, as&nbsp;</p>



<p><a href="https://archive.md/o/f5nIJ/https://www.merca2.es/2021/06/02/vtc-dentzel-tuenti-telefonica/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">published by Mercados magazine,</a>&nbsp;&nbsp;he has expanded his fortune thanks to VTC licenses.</p>



<hr class="wp-block-separator has-alpha-channel-opacity">



<figure class="wp-block-table"><table class="has-background" style="background-color:#f78da812"><tbody><tr><td>November 6, 2021</td><td>39 y/o trader</td><td>Hong Kong</td><td><a href="https://archive.is/OnZVR" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Crypto trader kidnapped by Triad gang, beaten with hammers</a></td></tr></tbody></table></figure>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full is-resized"><img decoding="async" loading="lazy" src="./All known physical attacks on Bitcoin and other cryptocurrencies from 2014 to 2022 - CRYPTO DEEP TECH_files/image-164.png" alt="All known physical attacks on Bitcoin and other cryptocurrencies from 2014 to 2022" class="wp-image-985" width="879" height="875" srcset="https://cryptodeeptech.ru/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/image-164.png 797w, https://cryptodeeptech.ru/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/image-164-300x300.png 300w, https://cryptodeeptech.ru/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/image-164-150x150.png 150w, https://cryptodeeptech.ru/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/image-164-768x765.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 879px) 100vw, 879px"></figure></div>


<p>Police have made a dramatic rescue of a cryptocurrency trader who was kidnapped by suspected triad members and held at a house in northern Hong Kong for nearly a week as his captors tried to extract a HK$30 million (US$3.85 million) ransom from his family.</p>



<p>Police raided the residence in the New Territories after being contacted by the family, and just as officers were swooping on the location, the trader managed to climb out a window and drop to the ground, the force revealed on Sunday.</p>



<p>But the kidnappers had beaten the victim, 39, with hammers in their unsuccessful attempt to force the ransom payment and he suffered leg fractures requiring hospital treatment, a source told the&nbsp;<em>Post</em>.</p>



<p>Officers arrested seven people and were hunting for about eight others, believed to be members of a Sun Yee On triad faction, including the suspected division boss.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image"><img decoding="async" src="./All known physical attacks on Bitcoin and other cryptocurrencies from 2014 to 2022 - CRYPTO DEEP TECH_files/ec9dd9ad437415049d65d7f1857bc5dc4c6066c7.webp" alt="Superintendent Alan Chung of Kowloon West regional crime unit. Photo: Handout"></figure>



<p>Superintendent Alan Chung of Kowloon West regional crime unit. Photo: Handout</p>



<p>Authorities were investigating whether any money was stolen from the man as he was forced to reveal the passwords for his bank and cryptocurrency accounts, acting Senior Superintendent Alan Chung of the Kowloon West regional crime unit said. According to the source, the digital currency holdings were worth more than HK$20 million.</p>



<p>“[After being rescued], the victim was unable to log on to his account with a cryptocurrency trading platform. We believe he suffered a loss,” Chung said. “We are still investigating.”</p>



<p>The victim’s ordeal began when he was lured into a Kowloon Bay industrial unit on November 6 for a transaction involving HK$4 million in Tether tokens.</p>



<p>But once inside, he was assaulted by several men. In the early hours of the next day, the trader was dragged into a car and driven to an unknown location where he was held in a container yard.</p>



<p>The criminals moved him the next day to the village house in Tai Po and placed him under heavy surveillance.</p>



<p>The source said he believed the man became a target because the triad gang suspected he was well-off, as he had a “supercar” worth millions of Hong Kong dollars.</p>



<p>But the insider clarified the man was neither famous nor extremely rich, and did not live in a luxury residence. However, he had made some money trading cryptocurrency, and liked to occasionally show off his earnings, including with the expensive car and various watches.</p>



<h3><strong><a href="https://archive.is/o/OnZVR/https://www.scmp.com/news/hong-kong/law-and-crime/article/3126660/hong-kong-thieves-bag-nearly-hk4-million-bogus-bitcoin?module=hard_link&amp;pgtype=article" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Hong Kong thieves bag nearly HK$4 million in bogus bitcoin transaction23 Mar 2021</a></strong></h3>



<p>“Kidnappers first demanded an HK$8 million ransom. It was raised to HK$30 million after they found out the victim had a lot of Tether tokens in his account,” the source said.</p>



<p>But despite intimidation from the criminals, the trader refused to call his family and ask them to pay the ransom, which triggered the beatings, according to the insider.</p>



<p>The family contacted authorities on Tuesday and the Kowloon West regional crime unit began investigating.</p>



<p>Officers identified the house where they suspected the trader was being held and officers carried out the raid on Friday night. Chung said the victim managed to climb out of the window on the mezzanine-floor and fell to the ground before officers moved in.</p>



<p>Police arrested two men at the scene, and four others and a woman over the weekend. The suspects in the latest arrests were aged between 25 and 32, and were jobless or worked in the catering, beauty or transport industry. The woman is suspected to be the tenant of the house.</p>



<h3><strong><a href="https://archive.is/o/OnZVR/https://www.scmp.com/news/hong-kong/law-and-crime/article/3155859/cross-border-smuggling-gang-suffers-heavy-blow-hong?module=hard_link&amp;pgtype=article" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">3 arrested, HK$63 million of contraband seized in Hong Kong customs bust12 Nov 2021</a></strong></h3>



<p>The last known kidnapping involving such a large amount of money was in 2015 when Queenie Rosita Law, granddaughter of late textiles tycoon Law Ting-pong, was abducted from her house and held in a mountain cave before family members paid a HK$28 million ransom. One member of the gang was later jailed for 12 years.</p>



<p>Police warned the public to remain wary of strangers wanting to set up a meeting involving large amounts of money.</p>



<p>“There has been growing concern about criminals using different excuses to set up face-to-face meetings for potential transactions,” Chung warned.</p>



<p>He asked people to select credible platforms for cryptocurrency transactions and avoid carrying a large sum of cash during the transactions.</p>



<p></p>

<figure class="wp-block-table"><table class="has-background" style="background-color:#f78da812"><tbody><tr><td>November 12, 2021</td><td>GBTC Crypto Exchange</td><td>Barcelona, Spain</td><td><a href="https://archive.md/AsIGX" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Thieves rip bitcoin ATM from crypto store</a></td></tr></tbody></table></figure>



<p class="has-text-align-center has-large-font-size"><strong>Thieves rip bitcoin ATM from Barcelona crypto-store</strong></p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full is-resized"><img decoding="async" loading="lazy" src="./All known physical attacks on Bitcoin and other cryptocurrencies from 2014 to 2022 - CRYPTO DEEP TECH_files/image-165.png" alt="All known physical attacks on Bitcoin and other cryptocurrencies from 2014 to 2022" class="wp-image-986" width="644" height="819" srcset="https://cryptodeeptech.ru/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/image-165.png 613w, https://cryptodeeptech.ru/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/image-165-236x300.png 236w" sizes="(max-width: 644px) 100vw, 644px"></figure></div>


<p>MADRID, Nov 12 (Reuters) – Spanish police are investigating the robbery of a ‘bitcoin ATM’ in a raid on a cryptocurrency exchange outlet in a wealthy Barcelona neighbourhood, local media reported on Friday.</p>



<p>Bitcoin ATMs allow customers to purchase cryptocurrency using cash or a debit card, while some also let users to exchange their crypto holdings for cash.</p>



<p>According to data from the Coin ATM radar website, which tracks the location of crypto ATMs, Spain has 158 such machines, the highest number in Europe.</p>



<p>Catalonia’s Mossos d’Esquadra police force said an ATM had been stolen at around 3 a.m. and declined to provide any more information to avoid hindering the investigation.</p>



<p>Citing police sources, EFE news agency said thieves took the bitcoin ATM from a shop on Beethoven street in the Sarria area, home to a branch of the GBTC cryptocurrency exchange.</p>



<p>GBTC did not return multiple requests for comment and the police declined to confirm the exact location of the robbery.</p>



<p>An unverified video purporting to show the crime showed an SUV ramming into the closed shutters of the GBTC storefront before half a dozen or so people in hoods carried the cash machine into a second car waiting on the street.</p>



<p>One of the assailants sprayed a fire extinguisher at onlookers as the two cars sped off into the night.</p>



<p>Reporting by Nathan Allen; Editing by Toby Chopra</p>

<figure class="wp-block-table"><table class="has-background" style="background-color:#f78da812"><tbody><tr><td>December 11, 2021</td><td>Camilla Guadagnuolo &amp; Principe Nerini</td><td>Bali, Indonesia</td><td><a href="https://archive.is/KJO7s" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Robbers take $400K in cash &amp; bitcoin at knifepoint</a></td></tr></tbody></table></figure>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full is-resized"><img decoding="async" loading="lazy" src="./All known physical attacks on Bitcoin and other cryptocurrencies from 2014 to 2022 - CRYPTO DEEP TECH_files/image-166.png" alt="All known physical attacks on Bitcoin and other cryptocurrencies from 2014 to 2022" class="wp-image-989" width="862" height="804" srcset="https://cryptodeeptech.ru/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/image-166.png 674w, https://cryptodeeptech.ru/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/image-166-300x280.png 300w" sizes="(max-width: 862px) 100vw, 862px"></figure></div>


<p>Denpasar, CNN Indonesia —&nbsp;</p>



<p>Petugas Polresta&nbsp;<strong><a href="https://archive.is/o/KJO7s/https://www.cnnindonesia.com/tag/denpasar" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Denpasar</a></strong>, Bali, berhasil menangkap dua Warga Negara Asing (WNA) bernama Nicola asal Italia dan Gregory asal Inggris karena melakukan pencurian dan kekerasan (<strong><a href="https://archive.is/o/KJO7s/https://www.cnnindonesia.com/tag/pencurian" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">curas</a></strong>).</p>



<p>Mereka melakukan perampokan kepada warga asing yang merupakan suami-istri asal Italia bernama Camilla Guadagnuolo dan Principe Nerini.</p>



<p>“Untuk kerugian selain uang tunai ada bitcoin. Jadi totalnya kerugiannya Rp 5,8 miliar,” kata Kapolresta Denpasar Kombes Pol Jansen Avitus Panjaitan di Mapolresta Denpasar, Bali, Selasa (28/12).</p>



<p>Selain Nicola dan Gregory, polisi memasukkan dua nama WNA lainnya ke dalam Daftar Pencarian Orang (DPO) yang terlibat aksi curas tersebut yakni WN Polandia dan WN Rusia.</p>



<p>Jansen menerangkan peristiwa itu terjadi pada Kamis (11/12) lalu, sekitar pukul 03:00 Wita, di sebuah villa tempat menginap korban, di Jalan Nakula, Seminyak, Kecamatan Kuta, Kabupaten Badung, Bali.</p>



<p>Saat itu, istri korban terbangun karena mendengar suara ledakan dan saat terbangun korban sudah melihat suaminya disekap di kamar korban oleh para pelaku yang menggunakan pakaian serba hitam serta menggunakan sarung tangan dan penutup kepala.</p>



<p>Kemudian, korban ditodong menggunakan pisau lalu diikat di tangan dan kakinya serta dilakban mulut dan kakinya. Selama penyekapan korban dipukul para pelaku secara bergantian dengan bertubi-tubi.</p>



<p>Lalu, salah satu pelaku mengambil enam ponsel korban dan satu ponsel lainnya yang berisi akun bitcoin korban dengan meminta&nbsp;<em>password</em>&nbsp;kepada korban.</p>



<p>“Dan apabila tidak diberitahu, maka pelaku akan membunuh istri korban dengan menempelkan pisau di leher istri korban. Dan selanjutnya korban memberi tahu&nbsp;<em>password</em>&nbsp;<em>handphone</em>&nbsp;tersebut,” katanya.</p>



<p>Dalam penyekapan yang dilakukan empat orang itu, korban mengetahui dua pelaku yaitu Nicola dan Gregory dari suaranya. Jansen mengatakan identitas pelaku dikenalinya karena Nicola merupakan mantan karyawan korban. Sementara, Gregory dikenali korban karena sempat mengikuti acara pesta di villa yang ditempati Nicola.</p>



<p>Setelah empat korban berhasil kabur, selanjutnya korban melaksanakan pengecekan terhadap akun bincance miliknya. Dan, diketahui ada perpindahan aset digital ke sebuah akun<em>&nbsp;wallet exodus</em>&nbsp;yang diduga milik pelaku Nicola yang dilakukan sebanyak tiga kali dengan total Rp5,8 miliar.</p>



<p>“Atas kejadian tersebut, kemudian korban melaporkannya ke Polsek Kuta. Modusnya, mereka berkelompok masuk ke rumah tersebut mengancam dan melakukan kekerasan terhadap korban dan mengambil uangnya,”&nbsp;ujar Jansen.</p>



<p>Dari laporan tersebut, polisi pun segera melakukan penyelidikan dan pemeriksaan CCTV&nbsp;hingga saksi di sekitar TKP.</p>



<p>Kemudian, pihak kepolisian berhasil menangkap pelaku Nicola di Jalan Raya Kerobokan, Badung, Bali, dan lalu menangkap pelaku Gregory yang tinggal bersama pacarnya di Jalan Setiabudi, Kuta, Bali.</p>



<p>Dari hasil pemeriksaan, Nicola mengaku melakukan aksi pencurian itu dengan Gregory dan Matt dan satu teman Matt yang belum dia kenal.</p>



<p>Kemudian, setelah melakukan aksinya Nicola dan Gregory kembali bertemu Matt bersama satu orang temannya yang tidak dikenal di satu tempat yang tidak diketahui. Kemudian Nicola mengambil salah satu walet yang berisi uang sebesar Rp 5,8 miliar yang merupakan uang digital bitcoin hasil pencurian milik korban dan satu walet berisi satu saldo lebih kecil untuk diserahkan kepada Matt dan temannya.</p>



<p>“Untuk motifnya memang tujuannya untuk mengambil harta dari korbannya. Untuk dua rekannya masih DPO satu dari Polandia dan satu lagi dari Rusia,” ujar Jansen.</p>



<hr class="wp-block-separator has-alpha-channel-opacity">



<figure class="wp-block-table"><table class="has-background" style="background-color:#f78da812"><tbody><tr><td>December 15, 2021</td><td>Vincent Everts</td><td>Amsterdam, Netherlands</td><td><a href="https://archive.md/tUbAz" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Armed home invaders threaten TV personality during livestream</a></td></tr></tbody></table></figure>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full"><img decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="1013" height="818" src="./All known physical attacks on Bitcoin and other cryptocurrencies from 2014 to 2022 - CRYPTO DEEP TECH_files/image-167.png" alt="All known physical attacks on Bitcoin and other cryptocurrencies from 2014 to 2022" class="wp-image-990" srcset="https://cryptodeeptech.ru/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/image-167.png 1013w, https://cryptodeeptech.ru/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/image-167-300x242.png 300w, https://cryptodeeptech.ru/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/image-167-768x620.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1013px) 100vw, 1013px"></figure></div>


<p>Trend watcher Vincent Everts was robbed at his house in Amsterdam at the end of the afternoon while he was in the middle of a live stream.&nbsp;On YouTube you can see how he abruptly disappears from view while he is talking with Maurice de Hond.”Fuck you! What is this now?”&nbsp;shouts Everts (video: see below).&nbsp;“What is it?”&nbsp;Someone outside the screen yells: “Bitcoin!”, to which Everts responds with: “I have no bitcoin at all.”&nbsp;He says to his interlocutors: “Someone is standing here now, someone is walking with a, um…”</p>



<h2>Gun to the head</h2>



<p>As soon as Everts has disappeared, Maurice de Hond asks if he should call the emergency number 112.&nbsp;Everts returns after a few minutes and says, visibly moved: “They pulled the camera away, put a gun to my head and said: Bitcoin! Bitcoin!”</p>



<h2>Trend watcher Vincent Everts robbed during livestream</h2>



<figure class="wp-block-embed aligncenter is-type-video is-provider-youtube wp-block-embed-youtube wp-embed-aspect-16-9 wp-has-aspect-ratio"><div class="wp-block-embed__wrapper">
<iframe loading="lazy" title="16:00 Live Q&amp;A @Mauricedehond @vincente evaluatie persconferentie! Plan voor nieuwe cabinet&amp; Overval" width="640" height="360" src="./All known physical attacks on Bitcoin and other cryptocurrencies from 2014 to 2022 - CRYPTO DEEP TECH_files/nEucOXglbLo.html" frameborder="0" allow="accelerometer; autoplay; clipboard-write; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture" allowfullscreen=""></iframe>
</div></figure>



<p>Everts told RTL Nieuws: “We are okay now. Three boys aged 20 or younger came in, one with a DHL shirt who pretended to deliver a package. They had a gun and demanded bitcoin. I refused, they pulled the camera out of the laptop I was live streaming with. I refused to cooperate and after a while of yelling they ran away.”</p>



<h2>‘Shoot’</h2>



<p>After he returned to the live stream, Everts told his interlocutors that the robbers also threatened his children and his wife.&nbsp;“At one point I said: shoot if you want. I clearly wasn’t going to cooperate and then they ran away. Then I called 911.”He says it’s “really insane” to have a gun pointed at you.&nbsp;“I’ve heard many times that people have been robbed because of bitcoin. I can’t reach that at all.”</p>

<p>According to police, it happened on Sunday at the Mobil gas station at 6133 Macon Rd.&nbsp;</p>



<p>The suspects used a gray 2004-2008 Ford F-150 and police said as of Monday, no arrests have been made.</p>



<p>If you have any information about the burglary, you can call Crime Stoppers anonymously at 901-528-CASH.</p>

<p>Burglary/Business Mobil Gas Station 6133 Macon Road Report #2201005957ME MEMPHIS, TN – On 1/16/22, officers were dispatched to an alarm call at 6133 Macon Road, Mobil Gas Station, upon arrival officers observed the front doors to be smashed down and the bitcoin ATM had been taken from the business. Suspects Vehicle: Gray 2004-2008 Ford F-150 Investigators need your help in identifying the individuals responsible. No arrest has been made. This is an ongoing investigation. Video of the suspects is attached. Anyone with information about this incident should call Crime Stoppers at 528-CASH. You will be given a secret ID number and your identification will remain completely anonymous. You can also submit your tip at http://www.crimestopmem.org where you will be able to review wanted fugitives and safely send investigators any helpful information on the suspect or suspects responsible for this crime. <figure class="aligncenter size-full is-resized"><img decoding="async" loading="lazy" src="./All known physical attacks on Bitcoin and other cryptocurrencies from 2014 to 2022 - CRYPTO DEEP TECH_files/image-171.png" alt="All known physical attacks on Bitcoin and other cryptocurrencies from 2014 to 2022" class="wp-image-999" width="879" height="1027" srcset="https://cryptodeeptech.ru/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/image-171.png 612w, https://cryptodeeptech.ru/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/image-171-257x300.png 257w" sizes="(max-width: 879px) 100vw, 879px"></figure></div>


<p>Mimoun ‘Mims’ Y. (32) and Mohamed EA (22) from Borgerhout were arrested when they tried to flee from the house in the&nbsp;</p>



<p><a href="https://archive.ph/o/LgqrJ/https://www.hln.be/antwerpen/leraar-34-en-moeder-thuis-overvallen-en-mishandeld-daders-willen-codes-van-kluis-met-3-miljoen-euro-aan-bitcoins~ab232aa8/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Hertog van Brabantlei in Hoboken on Friday morning.&nbsp;</a>The Rapid Response Team (SRT) was able to catch the two together with some police patrols.&nbsp;Later in the evening, a third suspect, a 23-year-old from Borsbeek, was arrested.&nbsp;The three were this morning before the council chamber on suspicion of theft with violence at night in a gang.&nbsp;The men were after cash, but when they couldn’t find it, they tried to empty the resident’s digital wallet.&nbsp;It did not work.&nbsp;The resident, a 34-year-old man, had a visit from his 61-year-old mother that morning.&nbsp;The two victims were treated harshly and had to be taken to hospital for treatment.&nbsp;</p>



<h2>“Needs a lot of research”</h2>



<p>The council chamber decided to extend the detention of the three suspects by one month.&nbsp;Lawyer Koen Vaneecke, who represents Mohamed EA, responded shortly after the courtroom: “My client is suspected of serious offences.&nbsp;His role and part will be further investigated and pending this he remains under further arrest.&nbsp;In any case, my client has never been convicted before.”A fourth suspect who was only arrested on Wednesday, a 29-year-old man from Deurne, will appear in court later.</p>
